# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="45bac-102">Types obsolètes dans le .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="45bac-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
